.search-page-header.wide .exposed-filters {
  background: none;
  padding: 0 0 0 12px;
  flex-grow: 0;
  /**** Filter popover width and positioning ****
                By default a popover will expand to match the size of the nearest ancestor with
                non-default positioning, which for these is the entire bar of filter buttons.
                In order to match the specs, we explicitly set the width of each popover.
                In order to keep the popover near the button but not flowing off the side of the screen
                we use the inherited value of 0 for right or left and set the other to auto to align the
                popover with the right or left edge of the filter buttons bar (which will always be
                fully on screen).
            */
}
.search-page-header.wide .exposed-filters .filter-buttons .filter-button-container {
  margin-right: 12px;
  /* end filter popover width and positioning */
  flex: none;
